#city_pd = pd.DataFrame(city_list) # Defining a DataFrame
#sampled_cities = city_pd.sample(1) # retrieving Sample of 500 City Names
#sampled_cities

# City_Name has been retrieved from http://bulk.openweathermap.org/sample/ 
# to avoid mismatch b/n citipy & Openweather API Data
file_path_city_list = os.path.join('city.list.json') # Defining 'json' file path
city_list_df = pd.read_json(file_path_city_list) # Reading a json file as a DataFrame
sample_cities = city_list_df['name'].sample(500) # Picking 500 sample cities
sample_cities.head()
city_list_df.head()

```python
# Save config information.
api_key = "bd180df6ce5cf274aa96746a4c1092eb"
url = "http://api.openweathermap.org/data/2.5/weather?"
units = "Imperial"

# Build partial query URL
query_url = url + "appid=" + api_key + "&units=" + units + "&q="

weather_data = [] # Initializing 'weather_data' as a list
cities = sample_cities # Assigning list of sample cities with the variable name 'cities'
count = 0 # Initializing count as 'Zero'

# Loop through the list of cities and perform a request for data on each
for city in cities:
    try:
        response = req.get(query_url + city).json()
        weather_data.append(response)
        count += 1
    except:
        print('oops! Something went wrong please check!')
    
    # Printing the above 'query_url' for each city name
    print("Processing record of %s" % str(count) + " of set %s" % str(len(cities)) + "| %s" % city + "\n" + query_url + city)   
```

# Finding number of responses with valid data

```python
weather_data.remove({'cod': '404', 'message': 'city not found'})
```


```python
# Deleting responses that are not containing 'City' name and other details
for response in weather_data:
    if(response['cod'] != 200):
        weather_data.remove({'cod': '404', 'message': 'city not found'})
```


```python
for response in weather_data:
    if(response['cod'] != 200):
        print(response)
```

len(weather_data)

    493




```python
# Retrieving specific data from 'weather_data' list with the above openweathermap API

lat_data = [data.get("coord").get("lat") for data in weather_data]
max_temp_data = [data.get("main").get("temp_max") for data in weather_data]
cloudiness_data = [data.get("clouds").get("all") for data in weather_data]
date_data = [data.get("dt") for data in weather_data]
humidity_data = [data.get("main").get("humidity") for data in weather_data]
lon_data = [data.get("coord").get("lon") for data in weather_data]
wind_speed_data = [data.get("wind").get("speed") for data in weather_data]
name_data = [data.get("name") for data in weather_data]
country_data = [data.get("sys").get("country") for data in weather_data]

# Creating a DataFrame from the above data lists    
weather_data = {"Max_Temp": max_temp_data, "Lat": lat_data, "Cloudiness": cloudiness_data, "Date": date_data,
                                    "Humidity": humidity_data, "Lon": lon_data, "Wind_Speed": wind_speed_data, "City": name_data,
                                    "Country": country_data}
    
weather_data = pd.DataFrame(weather_data)
weather_data.to_csv("Weather_data_API_HW.csv", index=False) # Writing the above 'weather_data' into csv file
weather_data
```

```python
# *** Latitude vs Temperature (F) ***
```


```python
time = datetime.now()
time.strftime('%x')
```




    '12/23/17'




```python
plt.figure(figsize = (10,8)) # Defining figure dimensions

plt.grid() # Defining grid

plt.title("City Latitude vs Temperature %s" % "(" + time.strftime('%x') + ")", fontsize='14') # Defining title
plt.xlabel("Latitude", fontsize='14') # Defining x-label
plt.ylabel("Temperature (F)", fontsize='14') # Defining y-label

plt.scatter(weather_data['Lat'], weather_data['Max_Temp'], marker="o", color="b", alpha=0.75)

plt.savefig("City Latitude vs Temperature.png") # Saving figure
plt.show() # Showing figure
```


![png](Python_APIs_HW_files/Python_APIs_HW_11_0.png)



```python
# *** Humidity (%) vs. Latitude ***
```


```python
plt.figure(figsize = (10,8)) # Defining figure dimensions

plt.grid() # Defining grid

plt.title("City Latitude vs Humidity %s" % "(" + time.strftime('%x') + ")", fontsize='14') # Defining title
plt.xlabel("Latitude", fontsize='14') # Defining x-label
plt.ylabel("Humidity (%)", fontsize='14') # Defining y-label

plt.scatter(weather_data['Lat'], weather_data['Humidity'], marker="o", color="b", alpha=0.75)

plt.savefig("City Latitude vs Humidity.png") # Saving figure
plt.show() # Showing figure
```


![png](Python_APIs_HW_files/Python_APIs_HW_13_0.png)

plt.figure(figsize = (10,8)) # Defining figure dimensions

```python
# *** Wind Speed (mph) vs. Latitude ***
```


```python
plt.figure(figsize = (10,8)) # Defining figure dimensions

plt.grid() # Defining grid

plt.title("City Latitude vs Wind Speed %s" % "(" + time.strftime('%x') + ")", fontsize='14') # Defining title
plt.xlabel("Latitude", fontsize='14') # Defining x-label
plt.ylabel("Wind Speed (mph)", fontsize='14') # Defining y-label

plt.scatter(weather_data['Lat'], weather_data['Wind_Speed'], marker="o", color="b", alpha=0.75)

plt.savefig("City Latitude vs Wind Speed.png") # Saving figure
plt.show() # Showing figure
```
